# *the union* *has* <less than _num_> *thousand members* *in canada*.
# contradiction
# *the union*: the union; his cult; the biker club; the book club; 
# *has*: has; lost; kicked out; contacted; 
# *thousand members*: thousand members; complaints filed; dollars; worried workers; 
# *in canada*: in canada; with dues outstanding; on call; in retail alone; 

# args:  <<*the union* = the union>>  <<*has* = has>>  <<*thousand members* = complaints filed>>  <<*in canada* = in canada>> 
the union has more than 123 complaints filed in canada.
the union has less than 123 complaints filed in canada.
contradiction

# args:  <<*the union* = the union>>  <<*has* = has>>  <<*thousand members* = complaints filed>>  <<*in canada* = on call>> 
the union has more than 137 complaints filed on call.
the union has less than 137 complaints filed on call.
contradiction

# args:  <<*the union* = the union>>  <<*has* = has>>  <<*thousand members* = dollars>>  <<*in canada* = in canada>> 
the union has more than 158 dollars in canada.
the union has less than 158 dollars in canada.
contradiction

# args:  <<*the union* = the union>>  <<*has* = has>>  <<*thousand members* = worried workers>>  <<*in canada* = in canada>> 
the union has more than 135 worried workers in canada.
the union has less than 135 worried workers in canada.
contradiction

# args:  <<*the union* = the union>>  <<*has* = has>>  <<*thousand members* = worried workers>>  <<*in canada* = with dues outstanding>>

the union has less than 173 worried workers with dues outstanding.
